Plus, it also offers a vector graphics and flowcharts drawing program, a databases editor, and a Math formula editing application.\r\n\r\n*** File formats Ultra Office Suite can open\r\nUltra Office Suite can open a wide variety of file formats.\r\n\r\n- Opening text documents\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odt, .ott, .oth, .odm, .sxw, .stw, and .sxg ), Word Editor can open the following text document formats:\r\n• Microsoft Word 2007 - 2019 (.docx)\r\n• Microsoft Word 6.0/95/97/2000/XP (.doc and .dot)\r\n• Microsoft Word 2003 XML (.xml)\r\n• Microsoft Word 2007 XML (.docx, .docm, .dotx, .dotm)\r\n• Microsoft WinWord 5 (.doc)\r\n• WordPerfect Document (.wpd)\r\n• WPS 2000/Office 1.0 (.wps)\r\n• .rtf, .txt, and .csv\r\n• StarWriter formats (.sdw, .sgl, .vor)\r\n• DocBook (.xml)\r\n• Unified Office Format text (.uot, .uof)\r\n• Ichitaro 8/9/10/11 (.jtd and .jtt)\r\n• Hangul WP 97 (.hwp)\r\n• T602 Document (.602, .txt)\r\n• AportisDoc (Palm) (.pdb)\r\n• Pocket Word (.psw)\r\nWhen opening .htm or .html files (used for web pages), Ultra Office Suite customizes Writer for working with these files.\r\n\r\n- Opening spreadsheets\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.ods, .ots, .sxc and .stc), Excel Editor can open the following spreadsheet formats:\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2007 - 2019 (.xlsx)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 97/2000/XP (.xls, .xlw, and .xlt)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 4.x–5.0/95 (.xls, .xlw, and .xlt)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2003 XML (.xml)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2007 XML (.xlsx, .xlsm, .xltx, .xltm)\r\n• Microsoft Excel 2007 binary (.xlsb)\r\n• Lotus 1-2-3 (.wk1, .wks, and .123)\r\n• Data Interchange Format (.dif)\r\n• Rich Text Format (.rtf)\r\n• Text CSV (.csv and .txt)\r\n• StarCalc formats (.sdc and .vor)\r\n• dBASE (.dbf)\r\n• SYLK (.slk)\r\n• Unified Office Format spreadsheet (.uos, .uof)\r\n• .htm and .html files, including Web page queries\r\n• Pocket Excel (pxl)\r\n• Quattro Pro 6.0 (.wb2)\r\n\r\n- Opening presentations\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odp, .odg, .otp,.sxi, and .sti), PowerPoint Editor can open the following presentation formats:\r\n• Microsoft PowerPoint 2007 -
